   aviparyastenānuttarasaṃbodhipariṇāmitasakaladānādikuśalacaryāyām	aviparyastena anuttara saMboDi pariNAmita sakala dAna Adi kuSala caryAyAm
   aśeṣajagaduddharaṇe cābhiyuktne abhāvitavyam / yathoktam	aSeza jagat udDaraNe ca aBiyuktne aBAvitavyam / yaTA uktam
   āryadharmasaṃgītau 	Arya Darma saMgItO 
   māyākāro yathā kaścin nirmitaṃ moktumudyataḥ /	mAyA kAraH yaTA kaScid nirmitam moktum udyataH /
   na cāsya nirmite saṅgo jñātapūrvo yato 'sya saḥ //	na ca asya nirmite saFgaH jQAta pUrvaH yatas asya saH //
   tribhavaṃ nirmitaprakhyaṃ jñātvā saṃbodhipāragaḥ /	tri Bavam nirmita praKyam jQAtvA saMboDi pAragaH /
   sannahyanti jagaddhetoḥ jñātapūrve jage tathā // iti tasyaivaṃ /	sannahyanti jagat hetoH jQAta pUrve jage taTA // iti tasya evam /
   prajñām upāyaṃ ca satataṃ satkṛtyābhyasyataḥ krameṇa [cittaṃ]	prajQAm upAyam ca satatam satkRtya aByasyataH krameNa [cittaM]
   saṃtatiparipākād uttarottaraviśuddhataratamakṣaṇodayād	saMtati paripAkAt uttarottara viSudDataratama kzaNa udayAt 
   bhūtārthabhāvanāprakarṣaparyantagamena sakalakalpanājālarahitaṃ	BUta arTa BAvanA prakarza paryanta gamena sakala kalpanA jAla rahitam
   sphuṭataraṃ dharmadhātvadhigamaṃ vimalaṃ	sPuwataram DarmaDAtu aDigamam vimalam
   niścalanivātadīpavallokottarajñānam utpadyate / tadā ca	niScala nivAta dIpavat loka uttara jQAnam utpadyate / tadA ca
   vastuparyantatālambanam pratilabdhaṃ bhavati / darśanamārgaṃ ca praviṣṭo	vastu paryanta tA Alambanam pratilabDam Bavati / darSana mArgam ca pravizwaH 
   bhavati / prathamā ca bhūmiḥ prāptā bhavati / tatastaduttarā bhūmīḥ	Bavati / praTamA ca BUmiH prAptA Bavati / tatas tad uttarA BUmIH
   pariśodhayan krameṇa kanakavad aśeṣāvaraṇāpagame sati asaktam apratihataṃ	pariSoDayan krameNa kanaka vat aSeza AvaraNa apagame sati asaktam apratihatam
   jñānaṃ pratilabhya buddhabhūmim aśeṣaguṇādhārāṃ prāpto bhavati /	jQAnam pratilaBya budDa BUmim aSeza guNa ADArAm prAptaH Bavati /
   kāryapariniṣpattiṃ cālambanaṃ pratilabhate / tasmād buddhatvādhigamārthinā	kArya parinizpattim ca Alambanam pratilaBate / tasmAt budDa tva aDigama arTinA
   madhyamapaddhatau tāvad abhiyogaḥ karaṇīya iti /	maDyama padDatO tAvat aBiyogaH karaNIyaH iti /
   (Bhk 244)	(Bhj 244)
   prakāśya yat prāpi mayā śubham asamapaddhitam /	prakASya yat prApi mayA SuBam asama padDitam /
   puṇyamastu janastena prāpto madhyamapaddhitam //	puNyam astu janaH tena prAptaH maDyama padDitam //
   dūrīkṛterṣyādimalā hi santo guṇairatṛptāḥ salilairivābdhiḥ /	dUrIkRta IrzyAdi malAH hi santaH guNEH atRptAH salilEH iva abDiH /
   vivecya gṛṇhanti subhāṣitāni haṃsāḥ payo yatpayasi prahṛṣṭāḥ //	vivecya gRNhanti su BAzitAni haMsAH payaH yat payasi prahRzwAH //
   pakṣapātākulaṃ tasmād dūrīkṛtaṃ mano budhaiḥ /	pakzapAta Akulam tasmAt dUrIkRtam manaH buDEH /
   sarvameva grahītavyaṃ bālādapi subhāṣitam //	sarvam eva grahItavyam bAlAt api suBAzitam //
   ācāryakamalaśīlena ante nibaddho bhāvanākramaḥ samāptaḥ /	AcArya kamala SIlena ante nibadDaH BAvanA kramaH samAptaH /
   tṛtīyaḥ bhāvanākramaḥ samāptaḥ /	tRtIyaH BAvanA kramaH samAptaH /
